SECTION 2.2: TAILWIND CONFIGURATION
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

The tailwind.config.js should extend the default theme with custom values:

TAILWIND_CONFIG:
```javascript
/** @type {import('tailwindcss').Config} */
export default {
  content: [
    "./index.html",
    "./src/**/*.{js,ts,jsx,tsx}",
  ],
  theme: {
    extend: {
      colors: {
        primary: '#22c55e',        // Main brand color (customizable)
        secondary: '#e67e22',      // Secondary accent
        background: '#0f0f0f',     // Dark background
        surface: '#1a1a1a',        // Slightly lighter surface
        'text-primary': '#f5f0e8', // Light text
        'text-secondary': '#9ca3af', // Gray text
      },
      fontFamily: {
        display: ['"Bebas Neue"', 'sans-serif'],
        body: ['Inter', 'sans-serif'],
      },
      animation: {
        'float': 'float 6s ease-in-out infinite',
        'pulse-glow': 'pulse-glow 2s ease-in-out infinite',
        'spin-slow': 'spin 20s linear infinite',
      },
      keyframes: {
        float: {
          '0%, 100%': { transform: 'translateY(0)' },
          '50%': { transform: 'translateY(-20px)' },
        },
        'pulse-glow': {
          '0%, 100%': { opacity: 0.5, transform: 'scale(1)' },
          '50%': { opacity: 1, transform: 'scale(1.05)' },
        },
      },
      backdropBlur: {
        xs: '2px',
      },
      perspective: {
        '1000': '1000px',
        '1500': '1500px',
        '2000': '2000px',
      },
    },
  },
  plugins: [],
}
```

```css
@tailwind base;
@tailwind components;
@tailwind utilities;

@import url('https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Bebas+Neue&family=Inter:wght@300;400;500;600;700;800;900&display=swap');

@layer base {
  html {
    scroll-behavior: smooth;
  }
  
  body {
    @apply bg-[#0f0f0f] text-white antialiased;
    font-family: 'Inter', sans-serif;
    overflow-x: hidden;
  }
  
  ::selection {
    @apply bg-green-500 text-black;
  }
  
  ::-webkit-scrollbar {
    width: 8px;
  }
  
  ::-webkit-scrollbar-track {
    @apply bg-transparent;
  }
  
  ::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb {
    @apply bg-white/20 rounded-full;
  }
  
  ::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb:hover {
    @apply bg-white/40;
  }
}

@layer components {
  .text-stroke-white {
    -webkit-text-stroke: 1px white;
  }
  
  .preserve-3d {
    transform-style: preserve-3d;
  }
  
  .perspective-1000 {
    perspective: 1000px;
  }
  
  .backface-hidden {
    backface-visibility: hidden;
  }
}

@layer utilities {
  .transform-gpu {
    transform: translateZ(0);
    will-change: transform;
  }
}
```

This section describes all reusable UI utility components that power the animations throughout
the website. Each component is meticulously detailed with its purpose, props, and implementation.

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 3.1: TiltCard Component
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

PURPOSE: Creates a 3D tilt effect on any card-like element that responds to mouse movement.
The card tilts in 3D space following the cursor position, with an optional spotlight effect.

VISUAL_BEHAVIOR:
- When mouse enters the card, it "lifts" slightly in 3D space
- As mouse moves within the card, it tilts towards the cursor
- A radial spotlight/gloss effect follows the mouse position
- On mouse leave, the card smoothly returns to its flat position
- Children content is translated slightly on the Z-axis for depth perception

PROPS_INTERFACE:
```typescript
interface TiltCardProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;      // Content to display inside the card
  className?: string;             // Additional CSS classes
  spotlightColor?: string;        // Color for the spotlight effect (default: "rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.15)")
}
```

FRAMER_MOTION_HOOKS_USED:
- useMotionValue: To track raw mouse X and Y positions
- useSpring: To smooth the mouse values with spring physics (stiffness: 500, damping: 100)
- useTransform: To convert mouse position to rotation angles (-15deg to 15deg)
- useMotionTemplate: To create dynamic CSS background gradients

IMPLEMENTATION_DETAILS:
1. useRef to get the card's DOM element
2. onMouseMove handler calculates mouse position relative to card center
3. Mouse X/Y values are set on motion values
4. Springs smooth the raw values for natural feel
5. useTransform maps smoothed values to rotation: 
   - mouseY maps to rotateX (inverse for natural tilt up/down)
   - mouseX maps to rotateY
6. Card uses transformStyle: "preserve-3d" and perspective for 3D effect
7. Children wrapped in translateZ(50px) for depth
8. Spotlight overlay uses radial-gradient centered on mouse position

SPRING_PHYSICS:
- Stiffness: 500 (responsive but not instant)
- Damping: 100 (smooth, no oscillation)
- Result: Natural, fluid tilt response

ROTATION_RANGE:
- rotateX: -15deg to 15deg (based on vertical mouse position)
- rotateY: -15deg to 15deg (based on horizontal mouse position)

SPOTLIGHT_GRADIENT:
```css
radial-gradient(
  800px circle at calc(50% + ${mouseX}px) calc(50% + ${mouseY}px),
  spotlightColor,
  transparent 80%
)
```

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 3.2: ZoomSection Component
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

PURPOSE: Creates a scroll-triggered entrance animation where content zooms in and fades in
as it enters the viewport. This is the primary entrance animation used throughout the site.

VISUAL_BEHAVIOR:
- Content starts scaled down to 92%, translated 50px down, and at 0 opacity
- When the element enters the viewport (with 50px margin), it animates to full scale/position
- Animation uses a custom bezier curve for a premium "ease out" feel
- Optional delay parameter for staggered animations
- Animation only plays once (viewport: { once: true })

PROPS_INTERFACE:
```typescript
interface ZoomSectionProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;  // Content to animate
  className?: string;         // Additional CSS classes
  delay?: number;            // Animation delay in seconds (default: 0)
  index?: number;            // Alternative index-based delay
}
```

ANIMATION_VALUES:
- Initial state: { opacity: 0, scale: 0.92, y: 50 }
- Animated state: { opacity: 1, scale: 1, y: 0 }
- Duration: 0.8 seconds
- Easing: [0.22, 1, 0.36, 1] (custom bezier curve - fast start, slow end)

VIEWPORT_SETTINGS:
- once: true (animation plays once, doesn't reverse)
- margin: "-50px" (triggers 50px before element enters viewport)

USAGE_PATTERN:
```jsx
<ZoomSection className="mb-20" delay={0.2}>
  <h2>Section Title</h2>
  <p>Section content...</p>
</ZoomSection>
```

STAGGER_PATTERN:
When multiple ZoomSections are siblings, use incrementing delays:
```jsx
<ZoomSection delay={0}>Content 1</ZoomSection>
<ZoomSection delay={0.1}>Content 2</ZoomSection>
<ZoomSection delay={0.2}>Content 3</ZoomSection>
```

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 3.3: ParallaxBackground Component
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

PURPOSE: Creates decorative background shapes that move at different speeds during scroll,
creating a parallax depth effect. Purely decorative, adds visual interest without blocking content.

VISUAL_BEHAVIOR:
- Multiple geometric shapes (circles, squares, dot grids) positioned absolutely
- Each shape moves at a different rate relative to scroll position
- Some shapes also rotate as the user scrolls
- Very low opacity (5-50%) to not distract from content
- All elements have pointer-events: none

SHAPES_INCLUDED:
1. Large stroked circle (left): Moves slow, rotates clockwise
2. Large stroked circle (right): Moves slow, rotates counter-clockwise
3. Dashed circle: Moves in reverse direction
4. Square: Moves fast, rotates 45 degrees
5. Dot grid (4x4): Moves slow, 20% opacity

SCROLL_TRANSFORM_MAPPINGS:
```typescript
const ySlow = useTransform(scrollYProgress, [0, 1], ["0%", "100%"]);
const yFast = useTransform(scrollYProgress, [0, 1], ["0%", "-100%"]);
const yReverse = useTransform(scrollYProgress, [0, 1], ["0%", "50%"]);
const rotate = useTransform(scrollYProgress, [0, 1], [0, 180]);
const rotateRev = useTransform(scrollYProgress, [0, 1], [0, -180]);
```

STYLING_DETAILS:
- All shapes use white/green colors with very low opacity
- Borders are thin (1px) for subtle effect
- Some shapes use dashed borders for variety
- Blur filters applied to some shapes for soft focus

POSITIONING:
- Shapes positioned at various vh/vw percentages
- Designed to not overlap critical content areas
- Absolute positioning within relative container
- z-index: 0 (behind all content)

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 3.4: InteractiveHeading Component
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

PURPOSE: Creates headings where each letter responds individually to mouse hover with a
lift and color change effect. Adds playful interactivity to section titles.

VISUAL_BEHAVIOR:
- Text appears normal initially
- When hovering over any letter, that specific letter:
  - Lifts up by 10px (translateY)
  - Scales up slightly (1.05x)
  - Changes color to primary (green)
  - Gains a text glow/shadow
- Smooth transitions on all properties
- Letters are separated into individual spans for targeting

PROPS_INTERFACE:
```typescript
interface InteractiveHeadingProps {
  text?: string;          // Legacy prop for simple text
  title?: string;         // Main heading text (takes precedence)
  subtitle?: string;      // Optional small text above heading
  align?: "left" | "center" | "right";
  className?: string;
}
```

LETTER_SPLITTING_LOGIC:
1. Text is split by spaces into words
2. Each word is wrapped in a span for proper spacing
3. Each character within a word is wrapped in InteractiveHoverLetter
4. Space handling: Each word span has mr-[0.25em] for natural spacing

INTERACTIVE_HOVER_LETTER_COMPONENT:
```typescript
const InteractiveHoverLetter: React.FC<{ children: string }> = ({ children }) => {
  const [hovered, setHovered] = useState(false);
  
  return (
    <span
      className="inline-block transition-all duration-200 cursor-pointer"
      onMouseEnter={() => setHovered(true)}
      onMouseLeave={() => setHovered(false)}
      style={{
        transform: hovered ? 'translateY(-10px) scale(1.05)' : 'translateY(0) scale(1)',
        color: hovered ? primaryColor : textColor,
        textShadow: hovered ? '0 0 40px rgba(34,197,94,0.6)' : 'none',
      }}
    >
      {children}
    </span>
  );
};
```

ALIGNMENT_HANDLING:
```typescript
const alignmentClasses = {
  left: "text-left items-start",
  center: "text-center items-center mx-auto",
  right: "text-right items-end ml-auto",
};
```

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 3.5: Magnetic Component
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

PURPOSE: Creates a magnetic attraction effect where elements slightly follow the mouse cursor
when it's nearby. Used for buttons and navigation elements to add subtle interactivity.

VISUAL_BEHAVIOR:
- Element stays in its normal position by default
- When mouse moves within the element, it shifts slightly toward the cursor
- Movement is dampened (0.5x) for subtle effect
- On mouse leave, element springs back to original position
- Uses spring physics for smooth, natural motion

PROPS_INTERFACE:
```typescript
interface MagneticProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  strength?: number;  // Movement multiplier (default: 30, not directly used in code)
}
```

IMPLEMENTATION:
```typescript
const Magnetic: React.FC<MagneticProps> = ({ children, strength = 30 }) => {
  const ref = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const [position, setPosition] = useState({ x: 0, y: 0 });

  const handleMouseMove = (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    const { clientX, clientY } = e;
    const { height, width, left, top } = ref.current?.getBoundingClientRect() || {};
    
    const x = clientX - (left + width / 2);
    const y = clientY - (top + height / 2);
    
    setPosition({ x: x * 0.5, y: y * 0.5 }); // 0.5 dampening factor
  };

  const handleMouseLeave = () => {
    setPosition({ x: 0, y: 0 });
  };

  return (
    <motion.div
      ref={ref}
      onMouseMove={handleMouseMove}
      onMouseLeave={handleMouseLeave}
      animate={{ x: position.x, y: position.y }}
      transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 150, damping: 15, mass: 0.1 }}
    >
      {children}
    </motion.div>
  );
};
```

SPRING_PHYSICS:
- Stiffness: 150 (responsive)
- Damping: 15 (slight overshoot for bounce)
- Mass: 0.1 (lightweight, quick reaction)

USAGE_PATTERN:
```jsx
<Magnetic>
  <button>Click Me</button>
</Magnetic>
```

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 3.6: ScrollRevealText Component
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

PURPOSE: Creates a character-by-character reveal animation based on scroll position. Each
character transitions from dim to bright as the section scrolls into view.

VISUAL_BEHAVIOR:
- Text starts with all characters at 10% opacity (dimmed)
- As user scrolls, characters progressively become 100% opacity
- Characters reveal sequentially from first to last
- Creates a "text appearing" or "filling in" effect
- Color also transitions from gray to white

PROPS_INTERFACE:
```typescript
interface ScrollRevealTextProps {
  children: string;        // Text content (must be string for character splitting)
  className?: string;
}
```

SCROLL_OFFSET_SETTINGS:
```typescript
const { scrollYProgress } = useScroll({
  target: element,
  offset: ['start 0.9', 'start 0.4'] // Starts 90% down viewport, ends at 40%
});
```

CHARACTER_ANIMATION_LOGIC:
1. Split text into individual characters
2. For each character, calculate its portion of the total animation:
   - start = charIndex / totalChars
   - end = start + (1 / totalChars)
3. Map scroll progress to opacity for each character:
   ```typescript
   const opacity = useTransform(scrollYProgress, [start, end], [0.1, 1]);
   ```
4. Handle spaces by rendering as &nbsp;

IMPLEMENTATION:
```typescript
const ScrollRevealText: React.FC<ScrollRevealTextProps> = ({ children, className = "" }) => {
  const element = useRef(null);
  const { scrollYProgress } = useScroll({
    target: element,
    offset: ['start 0.9', 'start 0.4']
  });

  const characters = children.split("");
  const totalChars = characters.length;

  return (
    <span ref={element} className={`inline-flex flex-wrap ${className}`}>
      {characters.map((char, i) => {
        const start = i / totalChars;
        const end = start + (1 / totalChars);
        const opacity = useTransform(scrollYProgress, [start, end], [0.1, 1]);
        
        return (
          <motion.span key={i} style={{ opacity }} className="inline-block">
            {char === " " ? "\u00A0" : char}
          </motion.span>
        );
      })}
    </span>
  );
};
```

SECTION 4.3: ROTATING CARD Component


PURPOSE: A 3D card that floats above content, responds to both scroll position and mouse movement,
flips to show front/back images, and travels across the screen as user scrolls.

FEATURES:
- Fixed positioning (travels with scroll)
- 3D flip animation (rotateY from 0 to 360 degrees)
- Mouse tilt effect (rotateX and rotateY based on cursor)
- Scroll-based position animation (moves left then right)
- Scroll-based tilt animation (rotateZ tilts based on position)
- Front and back faces with different content
- Glow effect that follows the card
- Fades out and becomes display:none after animation completes
- Hidden on mobile devices

SCROLL_WAYPOINTS:
- 0-1000px: Center (50vw)  Far Left (15vw), Y: 50vh  55vh
- 1000-1200px: Dwell at left position
- 1200-2400px: Far Left (15vw)  Right (65vw), Y: 55vh  62vh
- 2400px+: Scroll away (translateY based on scroll), fade out

MOUSE_TRACKING:
`````typescript
const mouseX = useMotionValue(0);
const mouseY = useMotionValue(0);

const mouseRotateXRaw = useTransform(mouseY, [-vh/2, vh/2], [25, -25]);
const mouseRotateYRaw = useTransform(mouseX, [-vw/2, vw/2], [-25, 25]);

const mouseRotateX = useSpring(mouseRotateXRaw, { stiffness: 100, damping: 20 });
const mouseRotateY = useSpring(mouseRotateYRaw, { stiffness: 100, damping: 20 });
`````

COMBINED_ROTATION:
`````typescript
// Reduce mouse tilt during scroll animation
const mouseTiltMultiplier = useTransform(scrollY, [0, 2400, 2600], [0.3, 0.3, 1]);
const dampedMouseRotateY = useTransform([mouseRotateY, mouseTiltMultiplier], 
  ([m, mult]) => m * mult);
const combinedRotateY = useTransform([scrollRotateY, dampedMouseRotateY], 
  ([s, m]) => s + m);
`````

SPRING_PHYSICS:
- stiffness: 30, damping: 40, mass: 1 (slow, smooth movement)

CARD_DIMENSIONS:
- Width: 340px, Height: 460px
- Rounded corners: 2xl (16px)
- Box shadow with 60px blur

FACE_STYLING:
- Front: Main image, gradient overlay, name text, arrow button
- Back: Secondary image, gradient overlay, "My Workspace" text
- Both faces use backface-visibility: hidden and rotateY(180deg) for back


SECTION 4.4: ABOUT Component


PURPOSE: Introduction section with scroll-based text reveal animation and animated statistics
counters. Uses a two-column layout with space for the RotatingCard on desktop.

FEATURES:
- Character-by-character scroll reveal for main text
- Animated number counters for statistics
- Gradient background blob decoration
- Sticky positioning for content
- CTA buttons with hover effects

SCROLL_TEXT_IMPLEMENTATION:
`````typescript
const ScrollText: React.FC<ScrollTextProps> = ({ text, className = '' }) => {
  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLSpanElement>(null);
  const { scrollYProgress } = useScroll({
    target: containerRef,
    offset: ['start 0.95', 'start 0.6'] // Fast reveal
  });

  const words = text.split(' ');

  return (
    <span ref={containerRef}>
      {words.map((word, wordIndex) => (
        <span key={wordIndex} className="inline-block mr-[0.25em]">
          {word.split('').map((char, charIndex) => {
            const totalChars = text.replace(/ /g, '').length;
            const charsBefore = words.slice(0, wordIndex).join('').length + charIndex;
            const start = charsBefore / totalChars;
            const end = (charsBefore + 1) / totalChars;
            
            return (
              <ScrollChar 
                key={charIndex}
                char={char}
                scrollProgress={scrollYProgress}
                start={start}
                end={end}
              />
            );
          })}
        </span>
      ))}
    </span>
  );
};

const ScrollChar = ({ char, scrollProgress, start, end }) => {
  const opacity = useTransform(scrollProgress, [start, end], [0.2, 1]);
  const color = useTransform(scrollProgress, [start, end], ['#4b5563', '#ffffff']);
  
  return (
    <motion.span style={{ opacity, color }} className="inline-block">
      {char}
    </motion.span>
  );
};
`````

ANIMATED_COUNTER:
- Uses useInView to trigger counting animation
- Counts from 0 to target value
- Duration: typically 2 seconds
- Supports suffix ("+", "K+", etc.)

STATS_DISPLAYED:
- Years Experience (e.g., 6+)
- Clients/Members Served (e.g., 150K+)
- Projects/Designs Completed (e.g., 140+)

LAYOUT:
- Grid: 1 column mobile, 12 columns desktop
- Left column (4 cols): Space for RotatingCard
- Right column (8 cols): All content

`````typescript
const mouseX = useMotionValue(0);

// Preview container
<motion.div
  className="fixed z-[100] pointer-events-none w-[200px] h-[140px] 
             rounded-xl overflow-hidden shadow-2xl border-2 border-green-500/30 
             hidden md:block"
  style={{
    left: smoothX,
    top: smoothY,
    translateX: 20,  // Offset from cursor
    translateY: 20,
  }}
  animate={{
    opacity: hoveredItem !== null ? 1 : 0,
    scale: hoveredItem !== null ? 1 : 0.8,
  }}
  transition={{ duration: 0.2 }}
>

    {hoveredItem !== null && (

        initial={{ y: "100%", opacity: 0 }}

</motion.div>
`````

`````typescript
const targetRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
const { scrollYProgress } = useScroll({ target: targetRef });

const totalWidth = images.length * 400;
const x = useTransform(scrollYProgress, [0, 1], [400, -totalWidth + 400]);
const smoothX = useSpring(x, { stiffness: 50, damping: 15, mass: 0.5 });
`````

- Inner: sticky, top-0, height: 100vh

PER_ITEM_3D_TRANSFORMS:
`````typescript
const GalleryItem = ({ src, index, containerX }) => {
  const offset = index * 400;
  const plateauSize = isMobile ? 200 : 50;
  
  const inputRange = [
    -offset - 700,      // Start entrance
    -offset - plateauSize, // Start plateau
    -offset + plateauSize, // End plateau
    -offset + 700       // End exit
  ];
  
  // 3D effects with plateau (holds steady when centered)
  const rotateY = useTransform(containerX, inputRange, [45, 0, 0, -45]);
  const z = useTransform(containerX, inputRange, [-300, 0, 0, -300]);
  const opacity = useTransform(containerX, inputRange, [0, 1, 1, 0]);
  const scale = useTransform(containerX, inputRange, [0.8, 1.15, 1.15, 0.8]);
  const y = useTransform(containerX, inputRange, [80, 0, 0, 80]);
  
  // ... render with these transforms
};
`````

MOBILE_HANDLING:
- 3D rotateY and scale disabled on mobile for performance
- Opacity and y transforms still active
- Plateau size increased for better centering behavior

BACKGROUND_TEXT_PARALLAX:
`````typescript
const textX = useTransform(scrollYProgress, [0, 1], ["0%", "50%"]);
const opacityText = useTransform(scrollYProgress, [0, 0.2, 0.8, 1], [0, 1, 1, 0]);
`````

SPOTLIGHT_EFFECT:
`````typescript
const Card = ({ item, index, onHover, onLeave }) => {
  const mouseX = useMotionValue(0);
  const mouseY = useMotionValue(0);

  function handleMouseMove({ currentTarget, clientX, clientY }) {
    const { left, top } = currentTarget.getBoundingClientRect();
    mouseX.set(clientX - left);
    mouseY.set(clientY - top);
  }

  return (
    <motion.div onMouseMove={handleMouseMove} className="relative">
      {/* Spotlight Effect */}
      <motion.div
        className="pointer-events-none absolute -inset-px rounded-xl 
                   opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition duration-300"
        style={{
          background: useMotionTemplate
            radial-gradient(
              650px circle at px px,
              15,
              transparent 80%
            )
          
        }}
      />
      {/* Card content */}
    </motion.div>
  );
};
`````

ANIMATED_BACKGROUND_BLOBS:
`````typescript
<motion.div
  animate={{
`````

SECTION 4.9: PROCESS / TIMELINE Component


PURPOSE: Vertical timeline showing workflow steps with scroll-animated progress line
and lighting effects on nodes.

- Alternating left/right layout on desktop (zigzag)

PROGRESS_LINE:
`````typescript
const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
const { scrollYProgress } = useScroll({
  target: containerRef,
  offset: ["start center", "end center"]
});

// Background line (gray)
<div className="absolute left-[19px] md:left-1/2 top-0 bottom-0 w-[2px] bg-white/10" />

// Active line (green, scales with scroll)
<motion.div
  style={{ scaleY: scrollYProgress }}
  className="absolute left-[19px] md:left-1/2 top-0 bottom-0 w-[2px] 
             bg-green-500 origin-top shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(34,197,94,0.8)]"
/>
`````

NODE_LIGHTING:
`````typescript
const StepCard = ({ step, index, progress, totalSteps }) => {
  const threshold = index / (totalSteps - 1);
  
  const isLit = useTransform(progress, (v) => v >= threshold - 0.05 ? 1 : 0);
  const color = useTransform(progress, (v) => 
    v >= threshold - 0.05 ? "#22c55e" : "#333");
  const shadow = useTransform(progress, (v) => 
    v >= threshold - 0.05 ? "0 0 20px #22c55e" : "none");
  const scale = useTransform(progress, (v) => 
    v >= threshold - 0.05 ? 1.2 : 1);
  
  return (
    <div className="relative">
      <div className="absolute w-10 h-10 rounded-full border-4 border-white/10">
        <motion.div
          style={{ backgroundColor: color, boxShadow: shadow, opacity: isLit, scale }}
          className="w-4 h-4 rounded-full"
        />
      </div>
      {/* Step content */}
    </div>
  );
};
`````

ALTERNATING_LAYOUT:
`````typescript
const isEven = index % 2 === 0;
<div className={lex }>
`````


SECTION 4.10: FAQ Component


PURPOSE: Expandable FAQ accordion with smooth height animations and rotating plus icon.

FEATURES:
- Single-open accordion behavior
- Plus icon rotates 45 to become X when open
- Smooth height animation with custom easing
- Border and text color changes based on state
- InteractiveHeading for section title

ACCORDION_ITEM:
`````typescript
const AccordionItem = ({ i, expanded, setExpanded, question, answer }) => {
  const isOpen = i === expanded;

  return (
    <motion.div initial={false} className="border-b border-white/10">
      <button
        onClick={() => setExpanded(isOpen ? false : i)}
        className="flex items-center justify-between w-full py-8 text-left group"
      >
        <span className="text-xl md:text-2xl font-bold text-gray-300 
                        group-hover:text-white transition-colors">
          {question}
        </span>
        <motion.span
          animate={{ rotate: isOpen ? 45 : 0 }}
          transition={{ duration: 0.3 }}
          className={p-2 rounded-full border 
                     }
        >
          <Plus size={24} />
        </motion.span>
      </button>
      
      <AnimatePresence initial={false}>
        {isOpen && (
          <motion.div
            initial="collapsed"
            animate="open"
            exit="collapsed"
            variants={{
              open: { opacity: 1, height: "auto", marginBottom: 32 },
              collapsed: { opacity: 0, height: 0, marginBottom: 0 }
            }}
            transition={{ duration: 0.3, ease: [0.04, 0.62, 0.23, 0.98] }}
          >
            <div className="text-gray-400 leading-relaxed text-lg max-w-3xl">
              {answer}
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>
    </motion.div>
  );
};
`````

`````typescript
adial-gradient(300px circle at px px, black, transparent),

adial-gradient(300px circle at px px, black, transparent)
`````

MAGNETIC_EMAIL:
`````typescript
const [position, setPosition] = useState({ x: 0, y: 0 });

const handleMouseMove = (e) => {
  if (ref.current) {
    const btnRect = ref.current.getBoundingClientRect();
    const btnX = e.clientX - (btnRect.left + btnRect.width / 2);
    const btnY = e.clientY - (btnRect.top + btnRect.height / 2);
    
    if (Math.abs(btnX) < 200 && Math.abs(btnY) < 200) {
      setPosition({ x: btnX, y: btnY });
    } else {
      setPosition({ x: 0, y: 0 });
    }
  }
};

<motion.div
  ref={ref}
  animate={{ x: position.x * 0.2, y: position.y * 0.2 }}
  transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 150, damping: 15, mass: 0.1 }}
>
  <a href="mailto:email@example.com">
    email@example.com
  </a>
</motion.div>
`````

                              PART 6: ANIMATION PATTERNS REFERENCE                                  
                              [Copy-Paste Code Snippets]                                            
                                                                                                    


This section provides ready-to-use animation code patterns for common effects.


PATTERN 6.1: ENTRANCE ANIMATIONS


FADE_UP:
`````typescript
<motion.div
  initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
  whileInView={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
  viewport={{ once: true }}
  transition={{ duration: 0.6, ease: "easeOut" }}
>
`````

FADE_IN_SCALE:
`````typescript
<motion.div
  initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.9 }}
  whileInView={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}
  viewport={{ once: true }}
  transition={{ duration: 0.8, ease: [0.22, 1, 0.36, 1] }}
>
`````

SLIDE_FROM_LEFT:
`````typescript
<motion.div
  initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -50 }}
  whileInView={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
  viewport={{ once: true }}
  transition={{ duration: 0.8, ease: [0.22, 1, 0.36, 1] }}
>
`````

STAGGERED_CHILDREN:
`````typescript
const container = {
  hidden: { opacity: 0 },
  show: {
    opacity: 1,
    transition: { staggerChildren: 0.1 }
  }
};

const item = {
  hidden: { opacity: 0, y: 20 },
  show: { opacity: 1, y: 0 }
};

<motion.div variants={container} initial="hidden" whileInView="show">
  {items.map(i => <motion.div key={i} variants={item} />)}
</motion.div>
`````


PATTERN 6.2: HOVER EFFECTS


SCALE_UP:
`````typescript
<motion.div whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }} whileTap={{ scale: 0.98 }}>
`````

TRANSLATE_UP:
`````typescript
<motion.div whileHover={{ y: -5 }} transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 300 }}>
`````

COLOR_CHANGE:
`````typescript
<motion.div whileHover={{ color: "#22c55e", textShadow: "0 0 20px rgba(34,197,94,0.5)" }}>
`````

GLOW_EFFECT:
`````typescript
<motion.div whileHover={{ boxShadow: "0 0 30px rgba(34,197,94,0.4)" }}>
`````


PATTERN 6.3: SCROLL-BASED ANIMATIONS


PARALLAX_Y:
`````typescript
const { scrollYProgress } = useScroll();
const y = useTransform(scrollYProgress, [0, 1], ["0%", "50%"]);

<motion.div style={{ y }}>
`````

SCALE_ON_SCROLL:
`````typescript
const { scrollYProgress } = useScroll({ target: ref });
const scale = useTransform(scrollYProgress, [0, 0.5, 1], [0.8, 1, 0.8]);

<motion.div ref={ref} style={{ scale }}>
`````

OPACITY_REVEAL:
`````typescript
const { scrollYProgress } = useScroll({ target: ref, offset: ["start 0.9", "start 0.5"] });
const opacity = useTransform(scrollYProgress, [0, 1], [0, 1]);

<motion.div ref={ref} style={{ opacity }}>
`````


PATTERN 6.4: SPRING PHYSICS PRESETS


SNAPPY (fast, responsive):
`````typescript
{ stiffness: 500, damping: 30, mass: 0.5 }
`````

SMOOTH (balanced):
`````typescript
{ stiffness: 150, damping: 25, mass: 1 }
`````

BOUNCY (playful):
`````typescript
{ stiffness: 200, damping: 10, mass: 0.5 }
`````

SLUGGISH (heavy, slow):
`````typescript
{ stiffness: 30, damping: 40, mass: 2 }
`````

MAGNETIC_BUTTON:
`````typescript
{ stiffness: 150, damping: 15, mass: 0.1 }
`````

CURSOR_FOLLOWING:
`````typescript
{ stiffness: 200, damping: 25 }
`````


                                                                                                    
                              PART 7: BEST PRACTICES & PERFORMANCE                                  
                              [Optimization Guidelines]                                             
                                                                                                    



SECTION 7.1: PERFORMANCE OPTIMIZATION


GPU_ACCELERATION:
- Always use transform properties (translateX, translateY, scale, rotate)
- Avoid animating width, height, top, left (causes layout reflow)
- Use will-change: transform for complex animations
- Add transform-gpu class for GPU acceleration

LAZY_LOADING:
- Use loading="lazy" on images below the fold
- Consider intersection observer for heavy components
- Load fonts asynchronously with display: swap

REDUCE_ON_MOBILE:
- Disable 3D transforms on mobile devices
- Reduce particle counts and animation complexity
- Use simpler spring physics (lower stiffness) for battery life

IMAGE_OPTIMIZATION:
- Use WebP format when possible
- Implement srcset for responsive images
- Compress images (aim for <100KB per image)
- Consider blur-up placeholder technique

CODE_SPLITTING:
- Lazy load sections below the fold
- Use dynamic imports for heavy components
- Split vendor bundles appropriately


SECTION 7.2: ACCESSIBILITY


MOTION_PREFERENCES:
`````typescript
const prefersReducedMotion = window.matchMedia('(prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)').matches;

<motion.div
  initial={prefersReducedMotion ? false : { opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
  animate={prefersReducedMotion ? {} : { opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
>
`````

KEYBOARD_NAVIGATION:
- All interactive elements should be focusable
- Visible focus indicators
- Skip navigation link for screen readers
- Proper heading hierarchy

COLOR_CONTRAST:
- Minimum 4.5:1 contrast ratio for text
- Minimum 3:1 for large text and icons
- Don't rely on color alone for information

ARIA_LABELS:
- Meaningful labels for interactive elements
- Proper role attributes
- Live regions for dynamic content


SECTION 7.3: SEO CONSIDERATIONS


META_TAGS:
`````html
<meta name="description" content="Your business description here...">
<meta name="keywords" content="relevant, keywords, here">
<meta property="og:title" content="Page Title">
<meta property="og:description" content="Description for social sharing">
<meta property="og:image" content="/path/to/social-image.jpg">
<meta name="twitter:card" content="summary_large_image">
`````

STRUCTURED_DATA:
- Add JSON-LD schema markup for your business type
- Include organization, localBusiness, or person schema
- Add breadcrumb schema for navigation

PERFORMANCE_METRICS:
- Aim for Core Web Vitals green scores
- LCP < 2.5s, FID < 100ms, CLS < 0.1
- Preload critical assets

SECTION 8.1: COMPLETE HERO COMPONENT CODE


`````typescript
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import { ArrowDown } from 'lucide-react';

// Simple hover letter component - handles individual letter hover state
const HoverLetter: React.FC<{ char: string; delay: number }> = ({ char, delay }) => {
  const [hovered, setHovered] = useState(false);

  return (
    <span
      className="inline-block transition-all duration-200 cursor-pointer"
      onMouseEnter={() => setHovered(true)}
      onMouseLeave={() => setHovered(false)}
      style={{
        transform: hovered ? 'translateY(-10px) scale(1.05)' : 'translateY(0) scale(1)',
        color: hovered ? '#22c55e' : '#f5f0e8',
        textShadow: hovered ? '0 0 40px rgba(34,197,94,0.6)' : 'none',
        animationDelay: `ms`,
      }}
    >
      {char}
    </span>
  );
};

              </p>
            </motion.div>
          ))}
        </motion.div>

        {/* CTA Button */}
        <motion.a
          href="#about"
          initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
          transition={{ delay: 1 }}
          className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 px-6 py-3 rounded-full text-sm font-medium transition-all"

            backgroundColor: '#22c55e',
            color: '#0f0f0f',
          }}
        >
          View My Work
          <ArrowDown size={16} />
        </motion.a>
      </motion.div>

    </section>
  );
};

            initial={{ opacity: 0, width: 0 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, width: '100%' }}
            transition={{ delay: 0.2, duration: 0.8, ease: [0.22, 1, 0.36, 1] }}
            className="overflow-hidden mb-1"
          >
            <motion.p
              initial={{ x: -20 }}
              animate={{ x: 0 }}
              transition={{ delay: 0.3, duration: 0.6 }}
              className="text-sm tracking-[0.5em] uppercase whitespace-nowrap"
              style={{
                color: '#22c55e',
                fontFamily: "'Inter', sans-serif",
                fontWeight: 500,
              }}
            >
              {'Graphic Designer'.split('').map((char, i) => (
                <motion.span
                  key={i}
                  initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
                  animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                  transition={{ delay: 0.3 + i * 0.03, duration: 0.3 }}
                  className="inline-block"
                >
                  {char === ' ' ? '\u00A0' : char}
                </motion.span>
              ))}
            </motion.p>
          </motion.div>

          <h1
            className="text-[15vw] font-black tracking-tighter leading-none select-none"
            style={{
              fontFamily: "'Bebas Neue', 'Inter', sans-serif",
              letterSpacing: '-0.02em',
              textShadow: '0 0 30px rgba(245, 240, 232, 0.4), 0 0 60px rgba(245, 240, 232, 0.2)',
            }}
          >
            {text.split('').map((char, i) => (
              <HoverLetter key={i} char={char} delay={i * 50} />
            ))}
          </h1>
        </div>
      </motion.div>

      {/* Center space left for RotatingCard component */}

      {/* Left Side - Skills (Animated) */}
      <motion.div
        initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -50 }}
        animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
        transition={{ delay: 0.5, duration: 0.8, ease: [0.22, 1, 0.36, 1] }}
        className="absolute left-12 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 z-20"
      >
        {[
          { title: 'UI/UX', delay: 0.6 },
          { title: 'Jersey', delay: 0.7 },
          { title: 'Thumbnail', delay: 0.8 },
        ].map((skill, index) => (
          <motion.div
            key={skill.title}
            initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -30, scale: 0.9 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0, scale: 1 }}
            transition={{ delay: skill.delay, duration: 0.5, ease: 'easeOut' }}
            whileHover={{ x: 10, scale: 1.05 }}
            className={`flex items-start gap-3  cursor-pointer`}
          >
            <motion.div
              className="w-3 h-3 mt-2"
              style={{ backgroundColor: '#22c55e' }}
              whileHover={{ scale: 1.3, boxShadow: '0 0 15px rgba(34,197,94,0.8)' }}
            />
            <div style={{ fontFamily: "'Bebas Neue', sans-serif" }}>
              <motion.p
                className="text-2xl tracking-wider uppercase"
                style={{ color: '#f5f0e8' }}
                whileHover={{ color: '#22c55e' }}
              >
                {skill.title}
              </motion.p>
              <motion.p
                className="text-2xl tracking-wider uppercase"
                style={{ color: '#f5f0e8' }}
                whileHover={{ color: '#22c55e' }}
              >
                Designer
              </motion.p>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        ))}
      </motion.div>

      {/* Right Side - Skills (Animated) */}
      <motion.div
        initial={{ opacity: 0, x: 50 }}
        animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
        transition={{ delay: 0.5, duration: 0.8, ease: [0.22, 1, 0.36, 1] }}
        className="absolute right-12 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 z-20 text-right"
      >
        {[
          { title: 'Graphic', delay: 0.6 },
          { title: 'Logo', delay: 0.7 },
          { title: 'Poster', delay: 0.8 },
        ].map((skill, index) => (
          <motion.div
            key={skill.title}
            initial={{ opacity: 0, x: 30, scale: 0.9 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0, scale: 1 }}
            transition={{ delay: skill.delay, duration: 0.5, ease: 'easeOut' }}
            whileHover={{ x: -10, scale: 1.05 }}
            className={`flex items-start gap-3 justify-end  cursor-pointer`}
          >
            <div style={{ fontFamily: "'Bebas Neue', sans-serif" }}>
              <motion.p
                className="text-2xl tracking-wider uppercase"
                style={{ color: '#f5f0e8' }}
                whileHover={{ color: '#e67e22' }}
              >
                {skill.title}
              </motion.p>
              <motion.p
                className="text-2xl tracking-wider uppercase"
                style={{ color: '#f5f0e8' }}
                whileHover={{ color: '#e67e22' }}
              >
                Designer
              </motion.p>
            </div>
            <motion.div
              className="w-3 h-3 mt-2"
              style={{ backgroundColor: '#e67e22' }}
              whileHover={{ scale: 1.3, boxShadow: '0 0 15px rgba(230,126,34,0.8)' }}
            />
          </motion.div>
        ))}
      </motion.div>

      {/* Bottom scroll indicator */}
      <motion.div
        initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
        animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
        transition={{ delay: 0.8 }}
        className="absolute bottom-8 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 z-20 flex flex-col items-center gap-3"
      >
        <ArrowDown size={14} className="text-gray-500 animate-bounce" />
      </motion.div>

      {/* Nav */}
      <div className="absolute top-6 right-12 z-30 flex gap-6">
        {['Home', 'About', 'Contact'].map((item) => (
          <a
            key={item}
            href={`#`}
            className="text-xs uppercase tracking-widest hover:opacity-60 transition-opacity"
            style={{ color: '#f5f0e8' }}
          >
            {item}
          </a>
        ))}
      </div>
    </section>
  );
};

// MAIN HERO - RENDERS MOBILE OR DESKTOP
// 
const Hero: React.FC = () => {
  return (
    <>
      <MobileHero />
      <DesktopHero />
    </>
  );
};

export default Hero;
`````
