────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 36.1: CONTENT SECURITY POLICY (CSP)
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Protect against XSS attacks with strict headers in `next.config.js`:

```javascript
const cspHeader = `
    default-src 'self';
    script-src 'self' 'unsafe-eval' 'unsafe-inline' https://va.vercel-scripts.com https://www.google-analytics.com;
    style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' https://fonts.googleapis.com;
    img-src 'self' blob: data: https://res.cloudinary.com https://*.google-analytics.com;
    font-src 'self' https://fonts.gstatic.com;
    object-src 'none';
    base-uri 'self';
    form-action 'self';
    frame-ancestors 'none';
    block-all-mixed-content;
    upgrade-insecure-requests;
`

module.exports = {
  async headers() {
    return [
      {
        source: '/(.*)',
        headers: [
          {
            key: 'Content-Security-Policy',
            value: cspHeader.replace(/\n/g, ''),
          },
        ],
      },
    ]
  },
}
```

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 36.2: INPUT VALIDATION WITH ZOD
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Always sanitize user input.
`npm install zod`

```typescript
import { z } from 'zod';

const contactSchema = z.object({
  name: z.string().min(2, "Name is too short"),
  email: z.string().email("Invalid email address"),
  message: z.string().min(10, "Message must be at least 10 characters").max(1000),
});

// Usage in handler:
const result = contactSchema.safeParse(req.body);
if (!result.success) {
  // Handle validation errors
  return res.status(400).json(result.error.format());
}
```

SECTION 37.1: GOOGLE ANALYTICS 4 STRATEGY
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Setup `lib/gtag.ts`:

```typescript
export const GA_TRACKING_ID = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_GA_ID;

// https://developers.google.com/analytics/devguides/collection/gtagjs/pages
export const pageview = (url: string) => {
  window.gtag('config', GA_TRACKING_ID, {
    page_path: url,
  });
};

// https://developers.google.com/analytics/devguides/collection/gtagjs/events
export const event = ({ action, category, label, value }: any) => {
  window.gtag('event', action, {
    event_category: category,
    event_label: label,
    value: value,
  });
};
```

Important Events to Track:
1. `download_resume`: Click on resume PDF.
2. `form_submit`: Successful contact inquiry.
3. `project_view`: Click on a portfolio case study.
4. `social_click`: Outbound click to LinkedIn/GitHub.
5. `scroll_depth`: User reaching 50%, 90% of page.

Automation is the key to velocity. This section defines the exact CI/CD pipelines needed to

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 39.1: GITHUB ACTIONS WORKFLOWS
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

WORKFLOW: CONTINUOUS INTEGRATION (ci.yml)
Runs on every pull request to verify code quality.

  name: CI Quality Assurance
  
  on:
    pull_request:
      branches: [main, develop]
    push:
      branches: [develop]

  jobs:
    validate:
      name: Validate Code
      runs-on: ubuntu-latest
      steps:
        - name: Checkout Repo
          uses: actions/checkout@v3
          
        - name: Setup Node
          uses: actions/setup-node@v3
          with:
            node-version: '18'
            cache: 'npm'
            
        - name: Install Dependencies
          run: npm ci
          
        - name: Lint Code
          run: npm run lint
          
        - name: Type Check
          run: npm run type-check
          
        - name: Run Unit Tests
          run: npm run test:unit
          
        - name: Check Formatting
          run: npm run format:check

    visual-regression:
      name: Visual Regression (Percy/Chromur)
      runs-on: ubuntu-latest
      needs: validate
      steps:
        - uses: actions/checkout@v3
        - uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        - run: npm ci
        - run: npm run build
        - run: npx playwright install --with-deps
        - run: npm run test:visual

WORKFLOW: PREVIEW DEPLOYMENT (preview.yml)
Deploys a preview environment for manual testing.

  name: Preview Deployment
  on:
    pull_request:
      types: [opened, synchronize]

  jobs:
    deploy-preview:
      runs-on: ubuntu-latest
      steps:
        - uses: actions/checkout@v3
        - uses: amondnet/vercel-action@v20
          with:
            vercel-token: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_TOKEN }}
            vercel-org-id: ${{ secrets.ORG_ID }}
            vercel-project-id: ${{ secrets.PROJECT_ID }}
            github-token: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 39.2: DOCKER CONTAINERIZATION
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

DOCKERFILE (Production Optimized):
For hosting outside of Vercel (e.g., AWS ECS, DigitalOcean).

  # Stage 1: Dependencies
  FROM node:18-alpine AS deps
  RUN apk add --no-cache libc6-compat
  WORKDIR /app
  COPY package.json package-lock.json ./
  RUN npm ci

  # Stage 2: Builder
  FROM node:18-alpine AS builder
  WORKDIR /app
  COPY --from=deps /app/node_modules ./node_modules
  COPY . .
  ENV NEXT_TELEMETRY_DISABLED 1
  RUN npm run build

  # Stage 3: Runner
  FROM node:18-alpine AS runner
  WORKDIR /app
  ENV NODE_ENV production
  ENV NEXT_TELEMETRY_DISABLED 1

  RUN addgroup --system --gid 1001 nodejs
  RUN adduser --system --uid 1001 nextjs

  COPY --from=builder /app/public ./public
  COPY --from=builder --chown=nextjs:nodejs /app/.next/standalone ./
  COPY --from=builder --chown=nextjs:nodejs /app/.next/static ./.next/static

  USER nextjs
  EXPOSE 3000
  ENV PORT 3000
  CMD ["node", "server.js"]

DOCKER-COMPOSE (Development):
  version: '3.8'
  services:
    web:
      build:
        context: .
        dockerfile: Dockerfile.dev
      ports:
        - "3000:3000"
      volumes:
        - .:/app
        - /app/node_modules
      environment:
        - NODE_ENV=development
    
    postgres:
      image: postgres:14-alpine
      ports:
        - "5432:5432"
      environment:
        POSTGRES_USER: user
        POSTGRES_PASSWORD: password
        POSTGRES_DB: portfolio_db

╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗

A professional website must be legally compliant. This section provides the legal text templates.
NOTE: These are templates and should be reviewed by legal counsel.

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 40.1: PRIVACY POLICY TEMPLATE
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Structure for `pages/privacy-policy.tsx`:

  **Last Updated:** [Date]

  **1. Introduction**
  Welcome to [Site Name] ("we," "our," or "us"). We are committed to protecting your privacy. This Privacy Policy explains how we collect, use, disclose, and safeguard your information when you visit our website [Website URL].

  **2. Information We Collect**
  We may collect information about you in a variety of ways. The information we may collect on the Site includes:

  *   **Personal Data:** Personally identifiable information, such as your name, shipping address, email address, and telephone number, and demographic information, such as your age, gender, hometown, and interests, that you voluntarily give to us when you register with the Site or when you choose to participate in various activities related to the Site.
  *   **Derivative Data:** Information our servers automatically collect when you access the Site, such as your IP address, your browser type, your operating system, your access times, and the pages you have viewed directly before and after accessing the Site.

  **3. Use of Your Information**
  Having accurate information about you permits us to provide you with a smooth, efficient, and customized experience. Specifically, we may use information collected about you via the Site to:
  *   Create and manage your account.
  *   Compile anonymous statistical data and analysis for use internally or with third parties.
  *   Email you regarding your account or order.
  *   Enable user-to-user communications.
  *   Fulfill and manage purchases, orders, payments, and other transactions utilizing the Site.

  **4. Disclosure of Your Information**
  We may share information we have collected about you in certain situations. Your information may be disclosed as follows:
  *   **By Law or to Protect Rights:** If we believe the release of information about you is necessary to respond to legal process, to investigate or remedy potential violations of our policies, or to protect the rights, property, and safety of others, we may share your information as permitted or required by any applicable law, rule, or regulation.
  *   **Third-Party Service Providers:** We may share your information with third parties that perform services for us or on our behalf, including payment processing, data analysis, email delivery, hosting services, customer service, and marketing assistance.

  **5. Tracking Technologies**
  We may use cookies, web beacons, tracking pixels, and other tracking technologies on the Site to help customize the Site and improve your experience. When you access the Site, your personal information is not collected through the use of tracking technology.

  **6. Security of Your Information**
  We use administrative, technical, and physical security measures to help protect your personal information. While we have taken reasonable steps to secure the personal information you provide to us, please be aware that despite our efforts, no security measures are perfect or impenetrable, and no method of data transmission can be guaranteed against any interception or other type of misuse.

  **7. Policy for Children**
  We do not knowingly solicit information from or market to children under the age of 13. If you become aware of any data we have collected from children under age 13, please contact us using the contact information provided below.

  **8. Contact Us**
  If you have questions or comments about this Privacy Policy, please contact us at:
  [Company Name]
  [Address]
  [Email Address]
  [Phone Number]

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 40.2: COOKIE CONSENT LOGIC (GDPR/CCPA)
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

COMPONENT: <CookieBanner />
  
  const [showBanner, setShowBanner] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    const consent = localStorage.getItem('cookie-consent');
    if (!consent) setShowBanner(true);
  }, []);

  const acceptCookies = () => {
    localStorage.setItem('cookie-consent', 'accepted');
    setShowBanner(false);
    // Initialize Analytics Here
    initializeGA();
  };

  const declineCookies = () => {
    localStorage.setItem('cookie-consent', 'declined');
    setShowBanner(false);
  };

  if (!showBanner) return null;

  return (
    <div className="fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 p-4 bg-neutral-900 border-t border-white/10 z-50">
      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto flex flex-col md:flex-row items-center justify-between gap-4">
        <p className="text-sm text-neutral-400">
          We use cookies to enhance your experience. By continuing to visit this site you agree to our use of cookies.
        </p>
        <div className="flex gap-4">
          <button onClick={declineCookies} className="text-sm text-neutral-400 hover:text-white">Decline</button>
          <button onClick={acceptCookies} className="text-sm bg-green-500 text-black px-4 py-2 rounded-full font-bold">Accept</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )

╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                                                    ║
║                              PART 41: LEGACY CODE MIGRATION & REFACTORING GUIDE                    ║
║                              [Moving from Old to New]                                              ║
║                                                                                                    ║
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

For users migrating from an existing WordPress or HTML site to this new React/Next.js architecture.

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 41.1: STRANGLER FIG PATTERN
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

STRATEGY:
Replace the old system piece by piece.

1.  **Deploy New Site to Subdomain:** `beta.yoursite.com`.
2.  **Reverse Proxy Configuration (Nginx/Vercel):** Route specific paths to the new app.
    
    // vercel.json
    {
      "rewrites": [
        { "source": "/blog/:path*", "destination": "https://old-wordpress-site.com/blog/:path*" },
        { "source": "/:path*", "destination": "/:path*" }
      ]
    }
3.  **Migrate Page by Page:**
    - Build "About" page in Next.js.
    - Update rewrite rule to stop proxying `/about`.
    - Repeat until everything is moved.

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 41.2: ASSET MIGRATION SCRIPT
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

NODE SCRIPT (migrate-images.js):
Downloads all images from old site and optimizes them.

  const fs = require('fs');
  const https = require('https');
  const path = require('path');
  
  const imageUrls = [/* List of 500+ URLs from old site */];
  const downloadDir = './public/migrated';

  if (!fs.existsSync(downloadDir)){
      fs.mkdirSync(downloadDir);
  }

  const download = (url, dest, cb) => {
    const file = fs.createWriteStream(dest);
    const request = https.get(url, (response) => {
      response.pipe(file);
      file.on('finish', () => {
        file.close(cb);
      });
    });
  };

  imageUrls.forEach((url, index) => {
    const filename = path.basename(url);
    download(url, path.join(downloadDir, filename), () => {
      console.log(`[${index}/${imageUrls.length}] Downloaded ${filename}`);
    });
  });

╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                                                    ║
║                              PART 42: EDGE COMPUTING & SERVERLESS ARCHITECTURE                     ║
║                              [Global Speed at Scale]                                               ║
║                                                                                                    ║
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

Leveraging the Edge allows us to run logic closer to the user, reducing latency to near zero.

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 42.1: EDGE MIDDLEWARE
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

GEOLOCATION BASED CONTENT:
Serve different content based on user country.

  // middleware.ts
  import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';

  export const config = {
    matcher: '/',
  };

  export function middleware(req: NextRequest) {
    const country = req.geo?.country || 'US';
    
    // Redirect logic
    if (country === 'DE') {
      return NextResponse.rewrite(new URL('/de', req.url));
    }
    
    // Header injection
    const response = NextResponse.next();
    response.headers.set('X-User-Country', country);
    return response;
  }

A/B TESTING AT THE EDGE:
Split traffic without client-side flicker.

  import { next } from '@vercel/edge';

  export default function middleware(req) {
    const bucket = Math.random() < 0.5 ? 'a' : 'b';
    const url = req.url;
    
    // Rewrite to the variant page
    req.nextUrl.pathname = `/${bucket}${req.nextUrl.pathname}`;
    return NextResponse.rewrite(req.nextUrl);
  }

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 42.2: SERVERLESS FUNCTIONS
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

IMAGE GENERATION (OG IMAGES):
Generate social card images on the fly using `@vercel/og`.

  // app/api/og/route.tsx
  import { ImageResponse } from 'next/og';
 
  export const runtime = 'edge';
 
  export async function GET(request: Request) {
    const { searchParams } = new URL(request.url);
    const title = searchParams.get('title') || 'My Portfolio';
 
    return new ImageResponse(
      (
        <div
          style={{
            display: 'flex',
            fontSize: 60,
            color: 'white',
            background: 'black',
            width: '100%',
            height: '100%',
            alignItems: 'center',
            justifyContent: 'center',
            flexDirection: 'column',
          }}
        >
          <h1>{title}</h1>
        </div>
      ),
      {
        width: 1200,
        height: 600,
      },
    );
  }

╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                                                    ║
║                              PART 43: CRISIS MANAGEMENT & INCIDENT RESPONSE                        ║
║                              [When Things Go Wrong]                                                ║
║                                                                                                    ║
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

Preparation for failure is the hallmark of a senior engineering approach.

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 43.1: DOWNTIME PLAYBOOK
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

SCENARIO 1: VERCEL OUTAGE
Status: Site returns 500 errors.
Action Plan:
1.  Check `status.vercel.com`.
2.  If critical, reroute DNS (Cloudflare) to backup S3 bucket / Netlify mirror.
3.  Post update to Twitter/Status Page.

SCENARIO 2: BAD DEPLOYMENT
Status: Bug in production.
Action Plan:
1.  Go to Vercel Dashboard -> Deployments.
2.  Find previous working deployment.
3.  Click "Instant Rollback".
4.  Investigation begins in `staging`.

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 43.2: SECURITY BREACH PROTOCOL
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

SCENARIO: API KEYS LEAKED
Action Plan:
1.  **Revoke Immediately:** Go to the provider (Supabase, OpenAI) and delete the leaked key.
2.  **Rotate Secrets:** Generate new keys and update Vercel Environment Variables.
3.  **Redeploy:** Trigger a redeploy to inject new env vars.
4.  **Audit:** Check logs for any unauthorized access during the leak window.

║                              PART 45: ADVANCED SECURITY HARDENING                                  ║
║                              [Fortress-Grade Protection]                                           ║
║                                                                                                    ║
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

Security is not an afterthought. It is baked into every layer of the application.

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 45.1: CONTENT SECURITY POLICY (CSP)
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

STRICT CONFIGURATION (next.config.js):
```javascript
const userSources = [
  '*.google-analytics.com',
  '*.googletagmanager.com',
  '*.youtube.com',
  '*.vimeo.com',
  '*.sanity.io'
];

const cspHeader = `
    default-src 'self';
    script-src 'self' 'unsafe-eval' 'unsafe-inline' ${userSources.join(' ')};
    style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline';
    img-src 'self' blob: data: ${userSources.join(' ')};
    font-src 'self';
    object-src 'none';
    base-uri 'self';
    form-action 'self';
    frame-ancestors 'none';
    block-all-mixed-content;
    upgrade-insecure-requests;
`;

module.exports = {
  async headers() {
    return [
      {
        source: '/(.*)',
        headers: [
          {
            key: 'Content-Security-Policy',
            value: cspHeader.replace(/\n/g, ''),
          },
        ],
      },
    ];
  },
};
```

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 45.2: INPUT SANITIZATION
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

ZOD SCHEMA VALIDATION:
Never trust user input. Validate everything on the server.

```typescript
import { z } from 'zod';

export const ContactFormSchema = z.object({
  name: z.string().min(2).max(50).trim().regex(/^[a-zA-Z\s]*$/, "No special characters allowed"),
  email: z.string().email().toLowerCase(),
  message: z.string().min(10).max(1000).trim().transform(val => escapeHtml(val)),
});

function escapeHtml(unsafe: string) {
  return unsafe
    .replace(/&/g, "&amp;")
    .replace(/</g, "&lt;")
    .replace(/>/g, "&gt;")
    .replace(/"/g, "&quot;")
    .replace(/'/g, "&#039;");
}
```

╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                                                    ║
║                              PART 47: ACCESSIBILITY (A11Y) MASTER PLAN                             ║
║                              [Inclusive Design for All]                                            ║
║                                                                                                    ║
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

Adherence to WCAG 2.1 AA standards is mandatory.

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 47.1: SCREEN READER OPTIMIZATION
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

ARIA LABELS:
Ensure all interactive elements lack text have labels.
`<button aria-label="Close Menu" className="icon-btn">X</button>`

SEMANTIC HTML:
Use `<main>`, `<nav>`, `<aside>`, `<article>`, `<header>`, `<footer>` appropriately.

SKIP LINKS:
First tab stop must be "Skip to Main Content".
`<a href="#main-content" className="sr-only focus:not-sr-only">Skip to content</a>`

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SECTION 47.2: KEYBOARD NAVIGATION
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

FOCUS TRAPPING (Modals):
When a modal is open, focus must not escape it.
Use `radix-ui/react-dialog` or `headlessui` which handles this automatically.

VISIBLE FOCUS INDICATORS:
Never use `outline: none` without providing a custom focus style.
`focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-green-500 focus-visible:ring-offset-2`

╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                                                                                                    ║
║                              PART 49: TROUBLESHOOTING & FAQS                                       ║
║                              [Developer Support]                                                   ║
║                                                                                                    ║
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

Common issues and their resolutions.

1. **Hydration Mismatch Errors:**
   - Cause: Server HTML differs from Client HTML.
   - Fix: Check for `typeof window !== 'undefined'` checks in render logic. Use `useEffect` for browser-only data.

2. **Framer Motion Jitter:**
   - Cause: Layout trashing.
   - Fix: Add `layout` prop to motion components or use `layoutId`.

3. **Images Not Loading:**
   - Cause: Domain not whitelisted in `next.config.js`.
   - Fix: Add hostname to `images.domains` config.

4. **Styles Not Applying:**
   - Cause: Tailwind not scanning files.
   - Fix: Check `content` array in `tailwind.config.js` to include all path aliases.
